2026-06-07 16:07:06.620 +05:30 [ERR] (24edc58e-a1d0-4ffe-b60c-a6d25f10018a) Failed executing DbCommand (38ms) [Parameters=[@warehouseId_Value='?' (DbType = Guid), @from_Value='?' (DbType = DateTime), @to_Value='?' (DbType = DateTime)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT s0."Date", CASE s0."MovementType"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Purchase'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Sale'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'TransferOut'
    WHEN 3 THEN 'TransferIn'
    WHEN 4 THEN 'Adjustment'
    WHEN 5 THEN 'Return'
    WHEN 6 THEN 'WriteOff'
    ELSE s0."MovementType"::text
END AS "MovementType", COALESCE(sum(s0."Quantity"), 0)::int AS "TotalQuantity", count(*)::int AS "TransactionCount"
FROM (
    SELECT s."MovementType", s."Quantity", date_trunc('day', s."CreatedAt", 'UTC') AS "Date"
    FROM stock_movements AS s
    WHERE s."WarehouseId" = @warehouseId_Value AND s."CreatedAt" >= @from_Value AND s."CreatedAt" <= @to_Value
) AS s0
GROUP BY s0."Date", s0."MovementType"
ORDER BY s0."Date"

2026-06-07 16:07:28.168 +05:30 [ERR] (146726ed-2382-4402-be7b-da79cd538d77) Failed executing DbCommand (3ms) [Parameters=[@warehouseId_Value='?' (DbType = Guid), @productId_Value='?' (DbType = Guid), @from_Value='?' (DbType = DateTime), @to_Value='?' (DbType = DateTime)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT s0."Date", CASE s0."MovementType"
    WHEN 0 THEN 'Purchase'
    WHEN 1 THEN 'Sale'
    WHEN 2 THEN 'TransferOut'
    WHEN 3 THEN 'TransferIn'
    WHEN 4 THEN 'Adjustment'
    WHEN 5 THEN 'Return'
    WHEN 6 THEN 'WriteOff'
    ELSE s0."MovementType"::text
END AS "MovementType", COALESCE(sum(s0."Quantity"), 0)::int AS "TotalQuantity", count(*)::int AS "TransactionCount"
FROM (
    SELECT s."MovementType", s."Quantity", date_trunc('day', s."CreatedAt", 'UTC') AS "Date"
    FROM stock_movements AS s
    WHERE s."WarehouseId" = @warehouseId_Value AND s."ProductId" = @productId_Value AND s."CreatedAt" >= @from_Value AND s."CreatedAt" <= @to_Value
) AS s0
GROUP BY s0."Date", s0."MovementType"
ORDER BY s0."Date"

    FROM goods_receipts AS g
    LEFT JOIN goods_receipt_items AS g0 ON g."Id" = g0."GoodsReceiptId"
) AS s4 ON s2."Id" = s4."PurchaseOrderId"
LEFT JOIN "SupplierInvoices" AS s1 ON s2."Id" = s1."PurchaseOrderId"
ORDER BY s2."Id", s2."Id0", s2."Id1", s3."Id", s3."Id0", s4."Id", s4."Id0"
